The bartender was more like a host, getting to know you, your taste, and very skilled at producing some of the most special, artisanal cocktails we've ever had.  Definitely worth it, if you can snag an invite.< /Review>

<review>The Modernist has some of the best cocktails in the city, if not the best. Carlo continues to astonish the locals with his new inventions for cocktails, adding in unique gold flakes, boba balls, and more.

If you are hosting a corporate event or birthday, they can make you your own private alcohol list, specific to the person or company, which adds a very nice touch.

Drinks are a bit on the pricier side as this is a very upscale venue that only uses the best liquor, which is warranted.

It is usually quiet enough to get a seat, but busy enough to create a good vibe.

Highly recommended for all to visit if you are in San Francisco if you are able to get an invite in.< /review><username>Albert K<//username><rate>5< /rate>< user>

<Name>Simon Holzman<//Name><time>1598627431285</time><Rate>5< /Rate><Text>We live in the mountains above Palm Desert where the temperature in the summer can hit 100 degrees and yet fall to 20 in the winter.

We had lived in our home for 15 years without quite being able to justify installing A/C since our Swamp Cooler coped reasonably well apart from about a month a year and we were out of the house during the days.

And then Covid hit and we were working from home and our Swamp Cooler simply couldn't do enough to make the 100 degree temperature during the day livable.

So, we asked Castillo Heating & Air Conditioning for some suggestions and a quote.

They proposed a Ductless three-way split system which would save us money on Propane during the winter months as well as cooling the house during the summer.

It took them two days to install it but they were quiet enough that we could work throughout with a minimum of disruption.

The ductless mini-split was amazing and made the temperature in the house much cooler. Indeed, my teenage daughter's room is like a morgue because she likes it really cool and keeps the door closed (did I mention "teenage").

However, the unit in the Master Bedroom was not performing as well as we would have liked. It was still acceptable to me, but my wife wasn't satisfied (I am not criticising her; she was right - I'm simply less aware of my environment than she is and didn't notice that it was closer to 80 than to the 75 it was set to). We called Castillo two times to look at it.

The first time, there was a genuine issue. One of the two fuses in the outside unit had blown and so it was running on half power. This was better than not running at all, I suppose, but the fact that it was running meant that we didn't have any reason to check the fuses. They replaced the fuse and assured us that it was very rare for them to blow like that and it was probably just a bad fuse in the first place. In the 6 weeks since then, the fuses have been fine despite a few power outages due to our Utility.

My wife was still unhappy and called Castillo's again. The chap that came examined everything again and was helpful and polite. Finally, he noticed that the vent in the Master Bedroom for the Swamp Cooler was still open and was about 4 foot above the ductless unit in that room. By checking with his thermometer, he found that the ductless unit was effectively sucking the air from outside through that vent. This was made worse by the fact that the swamp cooler is sort of above the outside condenser and so that air was extra warm.

He closed and covered that vent (and covered the other vents as well which were doubtless leaking air despite being closed) and, sure enough, it made a HUGE difference - Instead of being 78 degrees in the Master Bedroom, it was 68 last night ! (We have now set it to 75 and it's doing great.)

Thank you Castillo's for your hard work, your patience and your kindness when you must have been thinking that we were complete pains.

Very Highly Recommended.</Text>< pictures>
